\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ClearFromExpressionList()}{ClearFromExpressionList()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_luthetus_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_c_sharp_1_1_binder_case_1_1_c_sharp_binder_a75f612497ec229e20bd86692c12df6ee} 
void Luthetus.\+Compiler\+Services.\+CSharp.\+Binder\+Case.\+CSharp\+Binder.\+Clear\+From\+Expression\+List (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{interface_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_nodes_1_1_97d7489c2c3077ac339153787f61d38f}{IExpression\+Node}}}]{expression\+Node}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{interface_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_interfaces_1_1_i_parser_model}{IParser\+Model}}}]{model}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



A \doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_nodes_1_1_parenthesized_expression_node}{Parenthesized\+Expression\+Node} expression will "{}become"{} a \doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_nodes_1_1_comma_separated_expression_node}{Comma\+Separated\+Expression\+Node} upon encounter a \doxylink{struct_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_tokens_1_1_comma_token}{Comma\+Token} within its parentheses. 

An issue arises however, because the model.\+Expression\+List still says to "{}short circuit"{} when the \doxylink{struct_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_tokens_1_1_close_parenthesis_token}{Close\+Parenthesis\+Token} is encountered, and to at this point make the \doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_nodes_1_1_parenthesized_expression_node}{Parenthesized\+Expression\+Node} the primary expression.

Well, the \doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_nodes_1_1_parenthesized_expression_node}{Parenthesized\+Expression\+Node} should no longer exist, it was deemed to be more accurately described by a \doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_nodes_1_1_comma_separated_expression_node}{Comma\+Separated\+Expression\+Node}.

So, this method will remove any entries in the model.\+Expression\+List that have the \textquotesingle{}\doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_syntax_1_1_nodes_1_1_parenthesized_expression_node}{Parenthesized\+Expression\+Node}\textquotesingle{} as the to-\/be primary expression. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{_c_sharp_binder_8_expressions_8cs_source_l01565}{1565}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{_c_sharp_binder_8_expressions_8cs_source}{CSharp\+Binder.\+Expressions.\+cs}}.

\Hypertarget{class_luthetus_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_c_sharp_1_1_binder_case_1_1_c_sharp_binder_a735ec0eaca33905bfa8705cee069412c}\index{Luthetus.CompilerServices.CSharp.BinderCase.CSharpBinder@{Luthetus.CompilerServices.CSharp.BinderCase.CSharpBinder}!ClearStateByResourceUri@{ClearStateByResourceUri}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_luthetus_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_c_sharp_1_1_binder_case_1_1_c_sharp_binder_a735ec0eaca33905bfa8705cee069412c}

Do not invoke this when re-\/parsing the same file. 

Instead, only invoke this when the file is deleted, and should no longer be included in the binder.

Reason for this being\+: object initialization and collection initialization currently will at times break the \doxylink{class_luthetus_1_1_text_editor_1_1_razor_lib_1_1_compiler_services_1_1_implementations_1_1_parser}{Parser} for an entire file, and therefore they are much higher priority.
